{ ...initialEntry, timestamp: Date.now() } : null\n  );\n\n  // Push a new entry onto the stack\n  const push = useCallback((entry: NavEntry) => {\n    const newEntry = { ...entry, timestamp: Date.now() };\n    \n    if (current) {\n      setStack(prev => {\n        const newStack = [...prev, current];\n        // Limit history size\n        if (newStack.length > maxHistory) {\n          return newStack.slice(-maxHistory);\n        }\n        return newStack;\n      });\n    }\n    \n    setCurrent(newEntry);\n    onNavigate?.(newEntry, 'push');\n  }, [current, maxHistory, onNavigate]);\n\n  // Pop and return to the previous entry\n  const pop = useCallback((): NavEntry | null => {\n    if (stack.length === 0) return null;\n    \n    const newStack = [...stack];\n    const previous = newStack.pop()!;\n    \n    setStack(newStack);\n    setCurrent(previous);\n    onNavigate?.(previous, 'pop');\n    \n    return previous;\n  }, [stack, onNavigate]);\n\n  // Reset the stack to initial state\n  const reset = useCallback((entry?: NavEntry) => {\n    setStack([]);\n    setCurrent(entry ? { ...entry, timestamp: Date.now() } : null);\n  }, []);\n\n  // Replace current entry without affecting history\n  const replace = useCallback((entry: NavEntry) => {\n    setCurrent({ ...entry, timestamp: Date.now() });\n  }, []);\n\n  // Go back multiple steps\n  const goBackSteps = useCallback((steps: number): NavEntry | null => {\n    if (steps <= 0 || steps > stack.length) return null;\n    \n    const newStack = stack.slice(0, -steps);\n    const target = stack[stack.length - steps];\n    \n    setStack(newStack);\n    setCurrent(target);\n    onNavigate?.(target, 'pop');\n    \n    return target;\n  }, [stack, onNavigate]);\n\n  // Find an entry in history by id\n  const findInHistory = useCallback((id: string): NavEntry | null => {\n    if (current?.id === id) return current;\n    return stack.find(entry => entry.id === id) || null;\n  }, [current, stack]);\n\n  // Get breadcrumb trail\n  const breadcrumbs = useMemo(() => {\n    const trail = [...stack];\n    if (current) trail.push(current);\n    return trail;\n  }, [stack, current]);\n\n  // Check if we can go back\n  const canGoBack = stack.length > 0;\n\n  // Get history depth\n  const depth = stack.length + (current ? 1 : 0);\n\n  // Get the previous entry without popping\n  const previous = stack.length > 0 ? stack[stack.length - 1] : null;\n\n  return {\n    // State\n    current,\n    stack,\n    breadcrumbs,\n    previous,\n    depth,\n    canGoBack,\n    \n    // Actions\n    push,\n    pop,\n    reset,\n    replace,\n    goBackSteps,\n    findInHistory\n  };\n};\n\nexport default useNavStack;\n",

\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n\nimport React, { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';\n\ninterface VendorPhoneProps {\n  value: string;\n  onChange: (phone: string) => void;\n  onNext: () => void;\n  speak: (text: string) => void;\n  onVoiceDigits?: (handler: (digits: string) => void) => void;\n}\n\nconst THEME = { gold: '#B8860B', goldLight: '#F5EC9B' };\n\n// Format phone as 703-338-4931\nconst formatPhone = (digits: string): string => {\n  const clean = digits.replace(/\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\n  if (clean.length <= 3) return clean;\n  if (clean.length <= 6) return `${clean.slice(0, 3)}-${clean.slice(3)}`;\n  return `${clean.slice(0, 3)}-${clean.slice(3, 6)}-${clean.slice(6)}`;\n};\n\n// Speak phone as \"seven zero three \u2014 three three eight \u2014 four nine three one\"\nconst speakablePhone = (digits: string): string => {\n  const clean = digits.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n  const words: Record<string, string> = {\n    '0': 'zero', '1': 'one', '2': 'two', '3': 'three', '4': 'four',\n    '5': 'five', '6': 'six', '7': 'seven', '8': 'eight', '9': 'nine'\n  };\n  const digitWords = clean.split('').map(d => words[d] || d);\n  \n  if (clean.length >= 10) {\n    return `${digitWords.slice(0, 3).join(' ')} \u2014 ${digitWords.slice(3, 6).join(' ')} \u2014 ${digitWords.slice(6, 10).join(' ')}`;\n  }\n  return digitWords.join(' ');\n};\n\nconst VendorPhone: React.FC<VendorPhoneProps> = ({ \n  value, \n  onChange, \n  onNext, \n  speak,\n  onVoiceDigits \n}) => {\n  const [phone, setPhone] = useState(value);\n  const [confirmed, setConfirmed] = useState(false);\n  const [awaitingConfirmation, setAwaitingConfirmation] = useState(false);\n\n  // Update phone from parent value\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (value && value !== phone.replace(/-/g, '')) {\n      setPhone(formatPhone(value));\n    }\n  }, [value]);\n\n  // Handle voice digits\n  const handleVoiceDigits = useCallback((digits: string) => {\n    const newPhone = formatPhone(digits);\n    setPhone(newPhone);\n    onChange(digits.slice(0, 10));\n    \n    if (digits.length >= 10) {\n      // Ask for confirmation\n      setAwaitingConfirmation(true);\n      speak(`I heard: ${speakablePhone(digits)}. Is that correct? Say \"yes\" to confirm.`);\n    }\n  }, [onChange, speak]);\n\n  // Register voice digit handler\n  useEffect(() => {\n    onVoiceDigits?.(handleVoiceDigits);\n  }, [handleVoiceDigits, onVoiceDigits]);\n\n  // Handle typed input\n  const handleChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {\n    const digits = e.target.value.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n    const formatted = formatPhone(digits);\n    setPhone(formatted);\n    onChange(digits);\n    setAwaitingConfirmation(false);\n    setConfirmed(false);\n  };\n\n  // Handle confirmation\n  const handleConfirm = () => {\n    setConfirmed(true);\n    speak(`Perfect! Sending verification code to ${speakablePhone(phone.replace(/-/g, ''))}. For demo, use code 1 2 3 4 5 6.`);\n    setTimeout(onNext, 2000);\n  };\n\n  // Handle voice confirmation\n  const handleVoiceConfirm = useCallback((cmd: string) => {\n    if (awaitingConfirmation && phone.replace(/-/g, '').length >= 10) {\n      if (cmd.includes('yes') || cmd.includes('correct') || cmd.includes('confirm') || cmd.includes('right')) {\n        handleConfirm();\n      } else if (cmd.includes('no') || cmd.includes('wrong') || cmd.includes('change')) {\n        setAwaitingConfirmation(false);\n        setPhone('');\n        onChange('');\n        speak(\"No problem. Please say your phone number again, one digit at a time.\");\n      }\n    }\n  }, [awaitingConfirmation, phone, onChange, speak]);\n\n  const phoneDigits = phone.replace(/-/g, '');\n  const isValid = phoneDigits.length >= 10;\n\n  return (\n    <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\n      <span style={{ fontSize: '4em' }}>\ud83d\udcf1</span>\n      <h3 style={{ color: THEME.gold, marginTop: '16px', marginBottom: '8px' }}>\n        Enter Your Phone Number\n      </h3>\n      <p style={{ color: '#888', marginBottom: '24px', fontSize: '0.95em' }}>\n        Say it digit by digit, or type below\n      </p>\n      \n      {/* Phone Input */}\n      <div style={{ \n        display: 'flex', \n        alignItems: 'center', \n        justifyContent: 'center', \n        gap: '12px', \n        marginBottom: '20px' \n      }}>\n        <span style={{ \n          color: '#fff', \n          fontSize: '1.3em',\n          padding: '14px',\n          background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\n          borderRadius: '10px'\n        }}>\n          +1\n        </span>\n        <input\n          type=\"tel\"\n          value={phone}\n          onChange={handleChange}\n          placeholder=\"703-338-4931\"\n          style={{ \n            width: '220px', \n            padding: '18px', \n            fontSize: '1.4em', \n            borderRadius: '12px', \n            border: `2px solid ${isValid ? '#00ff00' : THEME.gold}`, \n            background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', \n            color: '#fff', \n            textAlign: 'center', \n            letterSpacing: '3px',\n            fontFamily: 'monospace',\n            transition: 'border-color 0.3s'\n          }}\n        />\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Status Message */}\n      {awaitingConfirmation && isValid && (\n        <div style={{\n          background: 'rgba(184,134,11,0.15)',\n          border: `1px solid ${THEME.gold}`,\n          borderRadius: '12px',\n          padding: '16px 24px',\n          marginBottom: '20px',\n          maxWidth: '350px',\n          margin: '0 auto 20px'\n        }}>\n          <p style={{ color: THEME.goldLight, margin: 0, fontSize: '0.95em' }}>\n            \ud83d\udcde <strong>{formatPhone(phoneDigits)}</strong>\n          </p>\n          <p style={{ color: '#aaa', margin: '8px 0 0', fontSize: '0.85em' }}>\n            Say \"yes\" to confirm or \"no\" to re-enter\n          </p>\n        </div>\n      )}\n\n      {/* Submit Button */}\n      <button\n        onClick={handleConfirm}\n        disabled={!isValid || confirmed}\n        style={{ \n          padding: '14px 40px', \n          background: isValid && !confirmed ? THEME.gold : '#444', \n          color: isValid && !confirmed ? '#000' : '#888', \n          border: 'none', \n          borderRadius: '25px', \n          cursor: isValid && !confirmed ? (digits: string): string => {\\n  const clean = digits.replace(/\\\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\\n  if (clean.length <= 3) return clean;\\n  if (clean.length <= 6) return `${clean.slice(0, one\\\"\\nconst speakablePhone = (digits: string): string => {\\n  const clean = digits.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n  const words: Record<string, string> = {\\n    '0': 'zero', '1': 'one', '2': 'two', '3': 'three', '4': 'four',\\n    '5': 'five', '6': 'six', '7': 'seven', '8': 'eight', '9': 'nine'\\n  };\\n  const digitWords = clean.split('').map(d => words[d] || d);\\n  \\n  if (clean.length >= 10) {\\n    return `${digitWords.slice(0, 3).join(' ')} \\u2014 ${digitWords.slice(3, 6).join(' ')} \\u2014 ${digitWords.slice(6, 10).join(' ')}`;\\n  }\\n  return digitWords.join(' ');\\n};\\n\\nconst VendorPhone: React.FC<VendorPhoneProps> = ({ \\n  value, \\n  onChange, \\n  onNext, \\n  speak,\\n  onVoiceDigits \\n}) => {\\n  const [phone, setPhone] = useState(value);\\n  const [confirmed, setConfirmed] = useState(false);\\n  const [awaitingConfirmation, setAwaitingConfirmation] = useState(false);\\n\\n  // Update phone from parent value\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (value && value !== phone.replace(/-/g, '')) {\\n      setPhone(formatPhone(value));\\n    }\\n  }, [value]);\\n\\n  // Handle voice digits\\n  const handleVoiceDigits = useCallback((digits: string) => {\\n    const newPhone = formatPhone(digits);\\n    setPhone(newPhone);\\n    onChange(digits.slice(0, 10));\\n    \\n    if (digits.length >= 10) {\\n      // Ask for confirmation\\n      setAwaitingConfirmation(true);\\n      speak(`I heard: ${speakablePhone(digits)}. Is that correct? Say \\\"yes\\\" to confirm.`);\\n    }\\n  }, [onChange, speak]);\\n\\n  // Register voice digit handler\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    onVoiceDigits?.(handleVoiceDigits);\\n  }, [handleVoiceDigits, onVoiceDigits]);\\n\\n  // Handle typed input\\n  const handleChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {\\n    const digits = e.target.value.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n    const formatted = formatPhone(digits);\\n    setPhone(formatted);\\n    onChange(digits);\\n    setAwaitingConfirmation(false);\\n    setConfirmed(false);\\n  };\\n\\n  // Handle confirmation\\n  const handleConfirm = () => {\\n    setConfirmed(true);\\n    speak(`Perfect! Sending verification code to ${speakablePhone(phone.replace(/-/g, ''))}. For demo, use code 1 2 3 4 5 6.`);\\n    setTimeout(onNext, 2000);\\n  };\\n\\n  // Handle voice confirmation\\n  const handleVoiceConfirm = useCallback((cmd: string) => {\\n    if (awaitingConfirmation && phone.replace(/-/g, '').length >= 10) {\\n      if (cmd.includes('yes') || cmd.includes('correct') || cmd.includes('confirm') || cmd.includes('right')) {\\n        handleConfirm();\\n      } else if (cmd.includes('no') || cmd.includes('wrong') || cmd.includes('change')) {\\n        setAwaitingConfirmation(false);\\n        setPhone('');\\n        onChange('');\\n        speak(\\\"No problem. Please say your phone number again, one digit at a time.\\\");\\n      }\\n    }\\n  }, [awaitingConfirmation, phone, onChange, speak]);\\n\\n  const phoneDigits = phone.replace(/-/g, '');\\n  const isValid = phoneDigits.length >= 10;\\n\\n  return (\\n    <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\\n      <span style={{ fontSize: '4em' }}>\\ud83d\\udcf1</span>\\n      <h3 style={{ color: THEME.gold, marginTop: '16px', marginBottom: '8px' }}>\\n        Enter Your Phone Number\\n      </h3>\\n      <p style={{ color: '#888', marginBottom: '24px', fontSize: '0.95em' }}>\\n        Say it digit by digit, or type below\\n      </p>\\n      \\n      {/* Phone Input */}\\n      <div style={{ \\n        display: 'flex', \\n        alignItems: 'center', \\n        justifyContent: 'center', \\n        gap: '12px', \\n        marginBottom: '20px' \\n      }}>\\n        <span style={{ \\n          color: '#fff', \\n          fontSize: '1.3em',\\n          padding: '14px',\\n          background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\\n          borderRadius: '10px'\\n        }}>\\n          +1\\n        </span>\\n        <input\\n          type=\\\"tel\\\"\\n          value={phone}\\n          onChange={handleChange}\\n          placeholder=\\\"703-338-4931\\\"\\n          style={{ \\n            width: '220px', \\n            padding: '18px', \\n            fontSize: '1.4em', \\n            borderRadius: '12px', \\n            border: `2px solid ${isValid ? THEME.gold : '#444', \\n          color: isValid && !confirmed ? '#000' : '#888', \\n          border: 'none', \\n          borderRadius: '25px', \\n          cursor: isValid && !confirmed ? specializes in curated ${category.toLowerCase()}${origin}, serving customers across ${regions} with fast, reliable delivery.\\n\\n\\u2728 **Why Choose Us:**\\n\\u2022 Premium quality products with attention to detail\\n\\u2022 Competitive pricing with transparent policies\\n\\u2022 Fast shipping and excellent customer service\\n\\n\\ud83d\\udce6 Shipping: ${regions}\\n\\ud83d\\udd12 Secure transactions guaranteed\\n\\u2b50 Customer satisfaction is our priority\\n\\n---\\n_Verified VistaView Partner_`;\\n};\\n\\nconst VendorProfile: React.FC<VendorProfileProps> = ({ \\n  profile, \\n  beautified, \\n  onChange, \\n  onBeautify, \\n  onSave, \\n  speak,\\n  onVoiceCommand \\n}) => {\\n  const [text, setText] = useState(profile);\\n  const [showBeautified, setShowBeautified] = voice commands\\n  const handleVoiceCommand = useCallback((cmd: string): boolean => {\\n    // Confirmation commands\\n    if (awaitingConfirmation) {\\n      if (cmd.includes('yes') || cmd.includes('change') || cmd.includes('edit') || cmd.includes('wrong')) {\\n        setShowBeautified(false);\\n        setAwaitingConfirmation(false);\\n        speak(\\\"No problem. Tell me what you'd like to change.\\\");\\n        return true;\\n      }\\n    }\\n    \\n    // If it's a long enough statement, treat it as profile input\\n    if (cmd.length > 30 && !cmd.includes('stop') && !cmd.includes('back') && !cmd.includes('close')) {\\n      setText(cmd);\\n      onChange(cmd);\\n      handleBeautify(cmd);\\n      return true;\\n    }\\n    \\n    return false;\\n  }, [awaitingConfirmation, onChange, onSave, speak]);\\n\\n  // Register voice handler\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    onVoiceCommand?.(handleVoiceCommand);\\n  }, [handleVoiceCommand, onVoiceCommand]);\\n\\n  // Beautify the profile\\n  const handleBeautify = (inputText?: string) => {\\n    const profileText = inputText || text;\\n    const fields = extractFields(profileText);\\n    setExtractedFields(fields);\\n    \\n    const beautifiedText = beautifyProfile(profileText, fields);\\n    onBeautify(beautifiedText);\\n    setShowBeautified(true);\\n    setAwaitingConfirmation(true);\\n    \\n    speak(\\\"Here's your beautified profile.   resize: 'vertical',\\n              fontSize: '1em',\\n              lineHeight: 1.6\\n            }}\\n          />\\n\\n          {text.length > 20 && (\\n            <div style={{ textAlign: For demo, enter 1 2 3 4 5 6.\");\n        }\n        return;\n      }\n    }\n\n    if (step === 'otp') {\n      const digits = extractDigits(cmd);\n      if (digits.length >= 1) {\n        voiceDigitHandlerRef.current?.(digits);\n        return;\n      }\n    }\n\n    if (step === 'profile') {\n      // Let profile component handle it\n      if (voiceCommandHandlerRef.current?.(cmd)) {\n        return;\n      }\n    }\n\n    if (step === 'dashboard') {\n      if (cmd.includes('upload') || cmd.includes('catalog') || cmd.includes('go live')) {\n        goToStep('upload', 'Upload');\n        voice.speak(\"Great! Upload your catalog. I'll process it and publish your products.\");\n        return;\n      }\n      if (cmd.includes('products') || cmd.includes('view')) {\n        voice.speak(\"Your product catalog will appear here after upload.\");\n        return;\n      }\n    }\n\n    if (step === 'complete') {\n      if (cmd.includes('view') || cmd.includes('products') || cmd.includes('catalog')) {\n        onComplete();\n        return;\n      }\n      if (cmd.includes('done') || cmd.includes('finish')) {\n        onClose();\n        return;\n      }\n    }\n\n  }, [step, vendorData.phone, onClose, onComplete]);\n\n  // Handle voice digits\n  const handleDigits = useCallback((digits: string) => {\n    voiceDigitHandlerRef.current?.(digits);\n  }, []);\n\n  const voice = useVoice({ \n    onCommand: handleCommand, \n    onDigits: handleDigits,\n    autoStart: isOpen \n  });\n\n  // Go back to previous step\n  const goBack = () => {\n    const stepOrder: Step[] = ['phone', 'otp', 'profile', 'dashboard', 'upload', 'pipeline'];\n    const idx = stepOrder.indexOf(step);\n    \n    if (idx === 0) {\n      onBack(); // Go back to role selection\n    } else {\n      const prev = stepOrder[idx - 1];\n      setStep(prev);\n      navStack.pop();\n      voice.speak(`Going back to ${STEPS.find(s => s.id === prev)?.label || prev}.`);\n    }\n  };\n\n  // Go to specific step\n  const goToStep = (newStep: Step, label: string) => {\n    navStack.push({ id: `vendor:${newStep}`, label });\n    setStep(newStep);\n  };\n\n  // Welcome message on open\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (isOpen && step === 'phone') {\n      setTimeout(() => {\n        voice.speak(\"Welcome, Vendor! For demo, enter 1 2 3 4 5 6.`);\n              }}\n              speak={voice.speak}\n              onVoiceDigits={(handler) => { voiceDigitHandlerRef.current = handler; }}\n            />\n          )}\n\n          {/* OTP Step */}\n          {step === 'otp' && (\n            <VendorOTP\n              onVerified={() => {\n                goToStep('profile', 'Profile');\n                voice.speak(\"Verified!
